e1000\+\_\+check\+\_\+reset\+\_\+block\+\_\+generic -\/ Check if P\+HY reset is blocked \+: pointer to the HW structure

Read the P\+HY management control register and check whether a P\+HY reset is blocked. If a reset is not blocked return E1000\+\_\+\+S\+U\+C\+C\+E\+SS, otherwise return E1000\+\_\+\+B\+L\+K\+\_\+\+P\+H\+Y\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+ET (12).

e1000\+\_\+determine\+\_\+phy\+\_\+address -\/ Determines P\+HY address. \+: pointer to the HW structure

This uses a trial and error method to loop through possible P\+HY addresses. It tests each by reading the P\+HY ID registers and checking for a match.

\index{e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+cable\+\_\+length\+\_\+igp\+\_\+2@{e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+cable\+\_\+length\+\_\+igp\+\_\+2}!e1000\+\_\+phy.\+h@{e1000\+\_\+phy.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+cable\+\_\+length\+\_\+igp\+\_\+2(struct e1000\+\_\+hw $\ast$hw)}{e1000_get_cable_length_igp_2(struct e1000_hw *hw)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf s32} e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+cable\+\_\+length\+\_\+igp\+\_\+2 (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{struct {\bf e1000\+\_\+hw} $\ast$}]{hw}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{e1000__phy_8h_a3348b159b99449955c582e0ecb9085bf}{}\label{e1000__phy_8h_a3348b159b99449955c582e0ecb9085bf}
e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+cable\+\_\+length\+\_\+igp\+\_\+2 -\/ Determine cable length for igp2 P\+HY \+: pointer to the HW structure

The automatic gain control (agc) normalizes the amplitude of the received signal, adjusting for the attenuation produced by the cable. By reading the A\+GC registers, which represent the combination of coarse and fine gain value, the value can be put into a lookup table to obtain the approximate cable length for each channel.

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+cable\+\_\+length\+\_\+m88(struct e1000\+\_\+hw $\ast$hw)}{e1000_get_cable_length_m88(struct e1000_hw *hw)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf s32} e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+cable\+\_\+length\+\_\+m88 (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{struct {\bf e1000\+\_\+hw} $\ast$}]{hw}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{e1000__phy_8h_a094e77497069b6c28af67c1bf77f2357}{}\label{e1000__phy_8h_a094e77497069b6c28af67c1bf77f2357}
e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+cable\+\_\+length\+\_\+m88 -\/ Determine cable length for m88 P\+HY \+: pointer to the HW structure

Reads the P\+HY specific status register to retrieve the cable length information. The cable length is determined by averaging the minimum and maximum values to get the \char`\"{}average\char`\"{} cable length. The m88 P\+HY has four possible cable length values, which are\+: Register Value Cable Length 0 $<$ 50 meters 1 50 -\/ 80 meters 2 80 -\/ 110 meters 3 110 -\/ 140 meters 4 $>$ 140 meters

e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+phy\+\_\+info\+\_\+82577 -\/ Retrieve I82577 P\+HY information \+: pointer to the HW structure

Read P\+HY status to determine if link is up. If link is up, then set/determine 10base-\/T extended distance and polarity correction. Read P\+HY port status to determine M\+D\+I/\+M\+D\+Ix and speed. Based on the speed, determine on the cable length, local and remote receiver.

e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+phy\+\_\+info\+\_\+igp -\/ Retrieve igp P\+HY information \+: pointer to the HW structure

Read P\+HY status to determine if link is up. If link is up, then set/determine 10base-\/T extended distance and polarity correction. Read P\+HY port status to determine M\+D\+I/\+M\+D\+Ix and speed. Based on the speed, determine on the cable length, local and remote receiver.

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+phy\+\_\+info\+\_\+m88(struct e1000\+\_\+hw $\ast$hw)}{e1000_get_phy_info_m88(struct e1000_hw *hw)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf s32} e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+phy\+\_\+info\+\_\+m88 (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{struct {\bf e1000\+\_\+hw} $\ast$}]{hw}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{e1000__phy_8h_a49cd2a3b0f7fc300b2fe19759d226a79}{}\label{e1000__phy_8h_a49cd2a3b0f7fc300b2fe19759d226a79}
e1000\+\_\+get\+\_\+phy\+\_\+info\+\_\+m88 -\/ Retrieve P\+HY information \+: pointer to the HW structure

Valid for only copper links. Read the P\+HY status register (sticky read) to verify that link is up. Read the P\+HY special control register to determine the polarity and 10base-\/T extended distance. Read the P\+HY special status register to determine M\+D\+I/\+M\+D\+Ix and current speed. If speed is 1000, then determine cable length, local and remote receiver.

Calls the P\+HY setup function to force speed and duplex. Clears the auto-\/crossover to force M\+DI manually. Waits for link and returns successful if link up is successful, else -\/\+E1000\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+P\+HY (-\/2).

e1000\+\_\+phy\+\_\+force\+\_\+speed\+\_\+duplex\+\_\+m88 -\/ Force speed/duplex for m88 P\+HY \+: pointer to the HW structure

Calls the P\+HY setup function to force speed and duplex. Clears the auto-\/crossover to force M\+DI manually. Resets the P\+HY to commit the changes. If time expires while waiting for link up, we reset the D\+SP. After reset, T\+X\+\_\+\+C\+LK and C\+RS on Tx must be set. Return successful upon successful completion, else return corresponding error code. 

e1000\+\_\+phy.\+c 파일의 1715 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

\index{e1000\+\_\+phy\+\_\+force\+\_\+speed\+\_\+duplex\+\_\+setup@{e1000\+\_\+phy\+\_\+force\+\_\+speed\+\_\+duplex\+\_\+setup}!e1000\+\_\+phy.\+h@{e1000\+\_\+phy.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{e1000\+\_\+phy\+\_\+force\+\_\+speed\+\_\+duplex\+\_\+setup(struct e1000\+\_\+hw $\ast$hw, u16 $\ast$phy\+\_\+ctrl)}{e1000_phy_force_speed_duplex_setup(struct e1000_hw *hw, u16 *phy_ctrl)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void e1000\+\_\+phy\+\_\+force\+\_\+speed\+\_\+duplex\+\_\+setup (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{struct {\bf e1000\+\_\+hw} $\ast$}]{hw, }
\item[{{\bf u16} $\ast$}]{phy\+\_\+ctrl}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{e1000__phy_8h_a24aa8f0dddd7bc3a882aed0b178c37c8}{}\label{e1000__phy_8h_a24aa8f0dddd7bc3a882aed0b178c37c8}
e1000\+\_\+phy\+\_\+force\+\_\+speed\+\_\+duplex\+\_\+setup -\/ Configure forced P\+HY speed/duplex \+: pointer to the HW structure \+: pointer to current value of P\+H\+Y\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+OL

Forces speed and duplex on the P\+HY by doing the following\+: disable flow control, force speed/duplex on the M\+AC, disable auto speed detection, disable auto-\/negotiation, configure duplex, configure speed, configure the collision distance, write configuration to C\+T\+RL register. The caller must write to the P\+H\+Y\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+OL register for these settings to take affect.

407         \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__osdep_8h_a3732dd7571f0d578b722df9d5a6e8c9a}{DEBUGOUT}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"I2CCMD Error bit set\(\backslash\)n"});
408         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a07c74865349e0dc0f182ff9f2d6a7a5c}{E1000\_ERR\_PHY};
409     \}
410 
411     \textcolor{comment}{/* Need to byte-swap the 16-bit value. */}
412     *data = ((i2ccmd >> 8) & 0x00FF) | ((i2ccmd << 8) & 0xFF00);
413 
414     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_ade686b442ce8b2b1dede6968fec28c10}{E1000\_SUCCESS};
415 \}

e1000\+\_\+read\+\_\+sfp\+\_\+data\+\_\+byte -\/ Reads S\+FP module data. \+: pointer to the HW structure \+: byte location offset to be read \+: read data buffer pointer

Reads one byte from S\+FP module data stored in S\+FP resided E\+E\+P\+R\+OM memory or S\+FP diagnostic area. Function should be called with \hyperlink{lib_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a0e19ca44ea3408780169ee2e75f096fb}{E1000\+\_\+\+I2\+C\+C\+M\+D\+\_\+\+S\+F\+P\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R($<$byte offset$>$)} for S\+FP module database access \hyperlink{lib_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a239eff1b62701690108ef8854ee20e1b}{E1000\+\_\+\+I2\+C\+C\+M\+D\+\_\+\+S\+F\+P\+\_\+\+D\+I\+A\+G\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R($<$byte offset$>$)} for S\+FP diagnostics parameters access

\index{e1000\+\_\+phy.\+h@{e1000\+\_\+phy.\+h}!e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d3\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+generic@{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d3\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+generic}}
\index{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d3\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+generic@{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d3\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+generic}!e1000\+\_\+phy.\+h@{e1000\+\_\+phy.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d3\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+generic(struct e1000\+\_\+hw $\ast$hw, bool active)}{e1000_set_d3_lplu_state_generic(struct e1000_hw *hw, bool active)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf s32} e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d3\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+generic (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{struct {\bf e1000\+\_\+hw} $\ast$}]{hw, }
\item[{{\bf bool}}]{active}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{e1000__phy_8h_aad37ac4e6b75dd59aabc421071162270}{}\label{e1000__phy_8h_aad37ac4e6b75dd59aabc421071162270}
e1000\+\_\+set\+\_\+d3\+\_\+lplu\+\_\+state\+\_\+generic -\/ Sets low power link up state for D3 \+: pointer to the HW structure \+: boolean used to enable/disable lplu

Success returns 0, Failure returns 1

The low power link up (lplu) state is set to the power management level D3 and Smart\+Speed is disabled when active is true, else clear lplu for D3 and enable Smartspeed. L\+P\+LU and Smartspeed are mutually exclusive. L\+P\+LU is used during Dx states where the power conservation is most important. During driver activity, Smart\+Speed should be enabled so performance is maintained.

e1000\+\_\+setup\+\_\+copper\+\_\+link\+\_\+generic -\/ Configure copper link settings \+: pointer to the HW structure

Calls the appropriate function to configure the link for auto-\/neg or forced speed and duplex. Then we check for link, once link is established calls to configure collision distance and flow control are called. If link is not established, we return -\/\+E1000\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+P\+HY (-\/2).

3333             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a07c74865349e0dc0f182ff9f2d6a7a5c}{E1000\_ERR\_PHY};
3334         mphy\_ctrl |= \hyperlink{e1000__phy_8h_accc51a14bb037daf595bb2bd8e673e1e}{E1000\_MPHY\_ENA\_ACCESS};
3335         \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__osdep_8h_a1abfc0be38040f1742629204b6e61865}{E1000\_WRITE\_REG}(hw, \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__regs_8h_a2ec3f5c7af40c1c7fbe94d0289650213}{E1000\_MPHY\_ADDR\_CTRL}, mphy\_ctrl);
3336     \}
3337 
3338     \textcolor{comment}{/* Set the address that we want to read */}
3339     ready = \hyperlink{e1000__phy_8c_a460d6eaf1ad17288fc2bbdea6b387061}{e1000\_is\_mphy\_ready}(hw);
3340     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!ready)
3341         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a07c74865349e0dc0f182ff9f2d6a7a5c}{E1000\_ERR\_PHY};
3342 
3343     \textcolor{comment}{/* We mask address, because we want to use only current lane */}
3344     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (line\_override)
3345         mphy\_ctrl |= \hyperlink{e1000__phy_8h_af4abba138289d507d183bbdb3de84fa3}{E1000\_MPHY\_ADDRESS\_FNC\_OVERRIDE};
3346     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
3347         mphy\_ctrl &= ~\hyperlink{e1000__phy_8h_af4abba138289d507d183bbdb3de84fa3}{E1000\_MPHY\_ADDRESS\_FNC\_OVERRIDE};
3348     mphy\_ctrl = (mphy\_ctrl & ~\hyperlink{e1000__phy_8h_a210ff678dcebdebc359a8773080133a2}{E1000\_MPHY\_ADDRESS\_MASK}) |
3349         (address & \hyperlink{e1000__phy_8h_a210ff678dcebdebc359a8773080133a2}{E1000\_MPHY\_ADDRESS\_MASK});
3350     \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__osdep_8h_a1abfc0be38040f1742629204b6e61865}{E1000\_WRITE\_REG}(hw, \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__regs_8h_a2ec3f5c7af40c1c7fbe94d0289650213}{E1000\_MPHY\_ADDR\_CTRL}, mphy\_ctrl);
3351 
3352     \textcolor{comment}{/* Read data from the address */}
3353     ready = \hyperlink{e1000__phy_8c_a460d6eaf1ad17288fc2bbdea6b387061}{e1000\_is\_mphy\_ready}(hw);
3354     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!ready)
3355         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a07c74865349e0dc0f182ff9f2d6a7a5c}{E1000\_ERR\_PHY};
3356     \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__osdep_8h_a1abfc0be38040f1742629204b6e61865}{E1000\_WRITE\_REG}(hw, \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a654a72cd2ce54597f3e19dec164cc565}{E1000\_MPHY\_DATA}, data);
3357 
3358     \textcolor{comment}{/* Disable access to mPHY if it was originally disabled */}
3359     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (locked)
3360         ready = \hyperlink{e1000__phy_8c_a460d6eaf1ad17288fc2bbdea6b387061}{e1000\_is\_mphy\_ready}(hw);
3361         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!ready)
3362             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a07c74865349e0dc0f182ff9f2d6a7a5c}{E1000\_ERR\_PHY};
3363         \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__osdep_8h_a1abfc0be38040f1742629204b6e61865}{E1000\_WRITE\_REG}(hw, \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__regs_8h_a2ec3f5c7af40c1c7fbe94d0289650213}{E1000\_MPHY\_ADDR\_CTRL},
3364                 E1000\_MPHY\_DIS\_ACCESS);
3365 
3366     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_ade686b442ce8b2b1dede6968fec28c10}{E1000\_SUCCESS};
3367 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

e1000\+\_\+write\+\_\+sfp\+\_\+data\+\_\+byte -\/ Writes S\+FP module data. \+: pointer to the HW structure \+: byte location offset to write to \+: data to write

Writes one byte to S\+FP module data stored in S\+FP resided E\+E\+P\+R\+OM memory or S\+FP diagnostic area. Function should be called with \hyperlink{lib_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a0e19ca44ea3408780169ee2e75f096fb}{E1000\+\_\+\+I2\+C\+C\+M\+D\+\_\+\+S\+F\+P\+\_\+\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R($<$byte offset$>$)} for S\+FP module database access \hyperlink{lib_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_a239eff1b62701690108ef8854ee20e1b}{E1000\+\_\+\+I2\+C\+C\+M\+D\+\_\+\+S\+F\+P\+\_\+\+D\+I\+A\+G\+\_\+\+A\+D\+D\+R($<$byte offset$>$)} for S\+FP diagnostics parameters access 

e1000\+\_\+phy.\+c 파일의 541 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.
